<user>108349327816470752803< /user><user_name>Melanie Tantingco<//user_name>< date>
1476649232430< /date>
<Rate>3<//Rate>< text>
Listen Up Peeps.  Was there on Saturday, 10/15/16 and was impress with most people, including clerk.  However, you will need to prepare:

1)  On Saturdays, ARRIVE EARLY (some arrive & wait as early as 4pm).  Mall Security allows people to wait inside starting at 8am, otherwise you must wait outside.  Believe me, they will kick you out.  Bring blanket, chairs, coffee, snacks, phone charger & reading material to keep comfortable & busy.
2)  Have you or someone BRING A PIECE OF PAPER and WRITE #1 thru #40 on each line.  This Passport Office generally serve 40 families per day.   Next to the #, have each person must write their names according to the order in which they arrive.
3)  Circulate the paper down the line until everyone writes their name.  Designate one person to manage it.  Note:  I arrived at 6:15am, and was #30 on the list.
FACT:  ONE LINE ITEM REPRESENTS ONE FAMILY whether its one, two or 5 family members.  Do not write individual names of your family member on separate lines.
5) COORDINATE with the person/people in front and the person managing the list, as well as, talk with the passport clerk to alert of the orderly & fair process created.
6)  At 10am, the passport office opens.  The passport clerk will post her own SIGN-UP LIST by the door.
TO KEEP FAIR & ORDER...we had the person who was managing the list & the people in front of the line to WRITE the first 40 people (from circulated list) on the PASSPORT CLERK LIST.  The passport clerk allowed us to write it as we explained to the clerk what we did & she honored the list circulated by the people....YEAH!
Passport Office closes for lunch from 1:00-2:00pm.
*BE AWARE THAT SOME PEOPLE IGNORE EVERYONE EFFORTS AND PUSH THEIR WAY NO MATTER WHAT.  Those people are deplorables & down right rude!!!!

Also, never hang out by the door.  It pisses the passport clerks and may delay or take their time, so stay by the hall.  Once your number has been written on the PASSPORT CLERK LIST, sit back and relax until your number is called.   The passport clerk may go through the number really fast, so as a suggestion, stay around & wait.  If they call your name & number and no response, you are automatically crossed off.
IF they have time at the end of the list, they MAY see you but its probably unlikely...just try and ask nicely.

After arriving at 6:15am & #30 on the list, I was done by 2:25pm.  It's an average of 10-15 minutes per family (person) if you have all your forms, photos, ID, etc completed and on hand.  Otherwise, it'll take longer.  Buckle down for a long day and please be patience.  Everyone is there for the same reason so CHILL.  Goodluck everyone!!!

BTW...bathrooms are open early by the Food Court and downstairs by Macys.<//text>
